# Progress

## 2026-07-11

### Retail Ops Share Links Phase 117 - Delivery Request Status Updates
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`; `brain/api/contracts.md`; `brain/database/schema.md`; `brain/modules/merchant-system.md`
- Completed: Added first-phase shared-link delivery request status updates. The DB layer now exposes `updateRetailOpsDeliveryRequestStatus`, which marks delivery requests assigned, picked up, delivered, or cancelled with the same selected-store and shared-link creator/admin scope as delivery request creation. Durable environments update `DeliveryRequest` status/timestamps, write a `TrackingEvent`, upsert or update the first self-delivery `DeliveryAssignment` summary for assigned/picked-up/delivered states, and mirror delivery plus fulfillment metadata back to the linked order. Undeployed environments update the existing `Order.metadata.retailOps.deliveryRequest` fallback. The API now exposes `retailOps.updateDeliveryRequestStatus` with optional status note, happened-at timestamp, and driver name/phone.
- Changed Source Files: `packages/db/src/queries/retail-ops-fulfillment.ts`, `apps/api/src/schemas/retail-ops.ts`, `apps/api/src/trpc/routers/retail-ops.ts`.
- Brain Files Updated: `brain/api/contracts.md`, `brain/api/endpoints.md`, `brain/api/permissions.md`, `brain/database/schema.md`, `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`, `brain/features/retail-ops-sales-product.md`, `brain/modules/merchant-system.md`, `brain/plans/2026-07-07-ux-ui-mobile-starter-dashboard.md`, `brain/progress.md`.
- Checks Run: targeted Biome check with formatter disabled for the fulfillment query, API schema, and Retail Ops router; single-file TypeScript compile probe for `packages/db/src/queries/retail-ops-fulfillment.ts`; tiny DB query import smoke; API schema import smoke; API router import smoke with placeholder `DATABASE_URL`; source marker scan for delivery status update symbols and Brain documentation; direct whitespace scan over touched code and Brain docs; scoped tracked diff check where Git has tracked paths.
- Skipped Checks Or Unresolved Issues: Did not run project-wide typecheck, dev servers, builds, migrations, database writes, broad tests, browser tests, live delivery status mutation, live mobile delivery UI, provider bidding/selection workflows, richer driver tracking views, provider-native webhook ingestion, provider-native online payment collection, migration application, or live DB validation because the fast Bun monorepo rule keeps this phase to scoped static verification unless heavier gates are explicitly requested.

### Retail Ops Share Links Phase 116 - First Delivery Request API Bridge
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`; `brain/api/contracts.md`; `brain/database/schema.md`; `brain/modules/merchant-system.md`
- Completed: Added the first protected delivery-request bridge for shared-link order follow-up. The DB layer now exposes `createRetailOpsDeliveryRequest` and `listRetailOpsDeliveryRequests`, creating order-linked `DeliveryRequest` rows with pickup/dropoff details when fulfillment tables are available and storing `Order.metadata.retailOps.deliveryRequest` as rollout fallback. Delivery reads return request status, pickup/dropoff contacts, customer/order/payment summary, share-link attribution, bid count, tracking-event count, and assignment summary when available. The API now exposes `retailOps.createDeliveryRequest` and `retailOps.deliveryRequests`, scoped so owner/admin/manager users can manage selected-store requests while cashier/operator users are limited to requests from links they created.
- Changed Source Files: `packages/db/src/queries/retail-ops-fulfillment.ts`, `packages/db/src/queries/index.ts`, `apps/api/src/schemas/retail-ops.ts`, `apps/api/src/trpc/routers/retail-ops.ts`.
- Brain Files Updated: `brain/api/contracts.md`, `brain/api/endpoints.md`, `brain/api/permissions.md`, `brain/database/schema.md`, `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`, `brain/features/retail-ops-sales-product.md`, `brain/modules/merchant-system.md`, `brain/plans/2026-07-07-ux-ui-mobile-starter-dashboard.md`, `brain/progress.md`.

- Skipped Checks Or Unresolved Issues: An additional single-file TypeScript probe for `apps/api/src/trpc/routers/retail-ops.ts` failed on existing unrelated issues at sync-event `never` inference around lines 941/944 and nullable arithmetic in `packages/utils/src/index.ts`; the new delivery-request symbols were not part of that failure. Did not run project-wide typecheck, dev servers, builds, migrations, database writes, broad tests, browser tests, live delivery-request creation, live mobile delivery UI, provider bidding/assignment/tracking workflows, delivery-state mutation workflow, provider-native webhook ingestion, provider-native online payment collection, migration application, or live DB validation because the fast Bun monorepo rule keeps this phase to scoped static verification unless heavier gates are explicitly requested.

### Retail Ops Share Links Phase 115 - Mobile Follow-Up Payment And Fulfillment Controls
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`; `brain/features/retail-ops-sales-product.md`; `brain/plans/2026-07-07-ux-ui-mobile-starter-dashboard.md`; `brain/modules/merchant-system.md`
- Completed: Added compact mobile follow-up controls for pending shared-link order requests. The mobile Product links sheet now lets permitted users choose cash, transfer, or card payment, choose ready-for-pickup, picked-up, or delivered fulfillment outcome, choose pickup or delivery method, and then complete the request with those fields sent to `retailOps.updateSharedLinkOrderRequestStatus`. Cancel still uses the cancellation path without payment fields, and the sheet keeps the existing offline/unavailable production fallbacks.

### Retail Ops Share Links Phase 114 - Fulfillment Outcome Follow-Up
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`; `brain/database/schema.md`; `brain/api/contracts.md`
- Completed: Added first-phase fulfillment outcome capture for shared-link follow-up. `retailOps.updateSharedLinkOrderRequestStatus` now accepts optional `fulfillmentStatus`, `fulfillmentMethod`, `fulfilledAt`, and `fulfillmentNote` fields alongside the existing completion/cancellation and paid follow-up fields. Completed requests can now store pickup/delivery outcome metadata with actor and timestamp; `picked_up` and `delivered` outcomes default the fulfilled timestamp to the follow-up time when omitted. Cancelled requests record a cancelled fulfillment outcome. Shared-link order request responses now include a normalized `fulfillment` summary so mobile/admin follow-up surfaces can show pickup/delivery state without creating a full dispatch/delivery request.
- Changed Source Files: `packages/db/src/queries/retail-ops-share-links.ts`, `apps/api/src/schemas/retail-ops.ts`, `apps/api/src/trpc/routers/retail-ops.ts`.

### Retail Ops Share Links Phase 113 - Paid Follow-Up Receipt Creation
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`; `brain/database/schema.md`; `brain/api/contracts.md`
- Completed: Added optional paid completion for shared-link order-request follow-up. `retailOps.updateSharedLinkOrderRequestStatus` now accepts optional `paymentMethod` (`cash`, `transfer`, or `card`), `cashierSessionId`, and `paidAt` fields. Completing a pending shared-link request with a payment method now creates a linked `Receipt`, marks the order `paymentStatus = PAID`, records `paymentState = paid_at_follow_up` plus payment/receipt metadata, still consumes the reserved stock, mirrors the completed/reservation state to durable share-link audit rows, and returns a receipt summary on shared-link order request responses. Completing without payment remains the existing follow-up-only path, and cancelling never creates a receipt.
- Changed Source Files: `packages/db/src/queries/retail-ops-share-links.ts`, `apps/api/src/schemas/retail-ops.ts`, `apps/api/src/trpc/routers/retail-ops.ts`.
- Brain Files Updated: `brain/database/schema.md`, `brain/api/contracts.md`, `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`, `brain/progress.md`.
- Checks Run: targeted Biome check with formatter disabled for the Retail Ops share-link query, API schema, and API router; single-file TypeScript compile probe for `packages/db/src/queries/retail-ops-share-links.ts` using a temporary `/private/tmp/ewatrade-node-crypto.d.ts` declaration because this workspace does not expose Node ambient types to ad hoc `tsc`; tiny DB package import smoke for `retail-ops-share-links.ts`; source marker scan for paid follow-up receipt symbols and Brain documentation; pending-placeholder scan; direct whitespace scan; scoped diff check over tracked touched docs.
- Skipped Checks Or Unresolved Issues: Did not run project-wide typecheck, dev servers, builds, migrations, database writes, broad tests, browser tests, live paid shared-link follow-up, mobile/web paid follow-up UI wiring, provider-native online payment collection, fulfillment, migration application, or live DB validation because the fast Bun monorepo rule keeps this phase to scoped static verification unless heavier gates are explicitly requested.

### Retail Ops Share Links Phase 112 - Provider Delivery Receipt And Retry Audit
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`; `brain/database/schema.md`; `brain/api/contracts.md`
- Completed: Added the first provider delivery receipt and retry audit bridge for shared-link notifications. Email transports can now return provider receipts, email dispatch returns per-recipient sent/failed results, and the notification email service preserves recipient role, subject, provider, provider message id, and failure details. Shared-link checkout now records successful enqueue as `queued` rather than `sent`; the background notification job records actual per-recipient delivery outcomes into order metadata and durable `ProductShareLinkNotification` rows, including attempt count, max attempts, next retry timestamp for all-recipient failures, provider ids, subjects, and failure reasons. Attempts where every shared-link email fails throw back into the existing job retry loop, while partial failures are audited without resending already-successful recipients in this bridge.
- Changed Source Files: `packages/email/src/index.ts`, `packages/notifications/src/services/email-service.ts`, `packages/jobs/src/handlers/notification-dispatch.ts`, `packages/jobs/src/index.ts`, `packages/db/src/queries/retail-ops-share-links.ts`, `apps/api/src/trpc/routers/retail-ops.ts`, `apps/storefront/src/app/p/[tenantSlug]/[storeSlug]/[productSlug]/page.tsx`.
- Brain Files Updated: `brain/database/schema.md`, `brain/api/contracts.md`, `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`, `brain/progress.md`.
- Checks Run: targeted Biome check with formatter disabled for the email package, notification email service, notification job handler/index, Retail Ops share-link query, API router, and storefront shared-product page; single-file TypeScript compile probe for `packages/db/src/queries/retail-ops-share-links.ts` using a temporary `/private/tmp/ewatrade-node-crypto.d.ts` declaration because this workspace does not expose Node ambient types to ad hoc `tsc`; email/notification import smoke; notification job handler import smoke with placeholder `DATABASE_URL`; DB share-link query import smoke; source marker scan for queued/provider receipt/retry symbols and Brain documentation; pending wording scan; direct whitespace scan; scoped diff check over tracked touched docs.
- Skipped Checks Or Unresolved Issues: Did not run project-wide typecheck, dev servers, builds, migrations, database writes, broad tests, browser tests, live provider delivery, live notification retry execution, live delivery validation, mobile/web notification retry UI, provider-native webhook receipt ingestion, real email provider configuration, payment, receipt creation, fulfillment, migration application, or live DB validation because the fast Bun monorepo rule keeps this phase to scoped static verification unless heavier gates are explicitly requested.

### Retail Ops Share Links Phase 111 - Durable Analytics Read Surface
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`; `brain/database/schema.md`; `brain/api/contracts.md`
- Completed: Added a protected durable share-link analytics read surface. The DB layer now exposes `getRetailOpsProductShareLinkAnalytics`, which uses the generated-link list as its scoped link population, reads `ProductShareLinkAnalyticsDaily` rows for a recent 30-day default or caller-supplied range, returns overall summary totals, per-link totals, and daily rows for views, unique visitors, order requests, follow-up outcomes, reservation quantities, consumed/released quantities, and completed revenue, and falls back to generated-link counters when the rollup table is unavailable. The tRPC router now exposes `retailOps.productShareLinkAnalytics` with store, date, product, and link filters plus report-history entitlement checks and cashier/operator creator scoping.

### Retail Ops Staff Profile Phase 104 - Durable Staff List Reads
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/plans/2026-07-06-feature-sales-rep-management-and-stock-wallets.md`; `brain/database/schema.md`
- Completed: Added durable-first staff profile reads. `retailOps.staff` now queries `RetailOpsStaffProfile` rows with user and membership snapshots when the staff-profile migration is available, maps them to the existing staff-list DTO, and then merges legacy `Membership`/`User` rows so owner/admin rows plus pre-cutover invited, active, or suspended staff remain visible during rollout. ### Retail Ops Billing Phase 83 - Normalized Provider Event Bridge

### Retail Ops Stock Phase 80 - Durable Adjustment Damage Loss Bridge
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/plans/2026-07-06-feature-stock-intake-and-unit-conversion-ledger.md`; `brain/api/contracts.md`
- Completed: Added the first durable stock adjustment, damage, and loss movement bridge. `retailOps.recordStockAdjustment` now rejects invalid reason/direction combinations before mutation, so damage/loss must decrease stock and found-stock must increase stock. External-id-backed adjustments can replay from durable movement rows when metadata fallback is missing, and successful adjustments mirror into one durable `InventoryMovement` row when the stock-ledger migration is available: `DAMAGE`/`LOSS` for those reasons, or `STOCK_ADJUSTMENT` for correction/found-stock, all with `STOCK_ADJUSTMENT` source, reason/source metadata, actor, note, happened-at timestamp, before/after balance, and movement group id. The API maps invalid adjustment requests to a bad-request response.
- Changed Source Files: `packages/db/src/queries/retail-ops-stock.ts`, `apps/api/src/trpc/routers/retail-ops.ts`.
- Brain Files Updated: `brain/api/contracts.md`, `brain/database/schema.md`, `brain/modules/merchant-system.md`, `brain/plans/2026-07-06-feature-stock-intake-and-unit-conversion-ledger.md`, `brain/progress.md`.

### Retail Ops Stock Phase 78 - Conversion Ratio Enforcement
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/plans/2026-07-06-feature-stock-intake-and-unit-conversion-ledger.md`; `brain/plans/2026-07-06-feature-flexible-product-units-and-price-history.md`; `brain/api/contracts.md`

### Retail Ops Stock Phase 48 - Reservation-Aware Central Decrements
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/api/contracts.md`; `brain/database/schema.md`; `brain/modules/merchant-system.md`; `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`
- Completed: Extended the first-phase shared-link stock reservation bridge across central stock decrement paths. Staff stock assignment now checks assignable central stock as `onHandQuantity - reservedQuantity` and uses an optimistic `reservedQuantity` guard before decrementing. Unit conversion now checks unreserved source stock and guards the source decrement against concurrent reservation changes. Manual stock adjustment decreases now require unreserved stock and use the same reserved-quantity guard. This keeps pending shared-link order reservations from being consumed by assignment, conversion, or manual decrease flows before the durable reservation table cutover lands.
- Changed Source Files: `packages/db/src/queries/retail-ops-stock-wallets.ts`, `packages/db/src/queries/retail-ops-stock.ts`.
- Brain Files Updated: `brain/api/contracts.md`, `brain/database/schema.md`, `brain/modules/merchant-system.md`, `brain/progress.md`.
- Checks Run: targeted Biome check with formatter disabled for the Retail Ops stock-wallet and stock query modules; targeted Bun imports for the stock-wallet and stock query modules; marker scan for reserved-stock guards in source and Brain docs; stale current-stock wording scan; copied-source drift scan; direct whitespace scan; scoped `git diff --check`.
- Skipped Checks Or Unresolved Issues: Did not run typecheck, Prisma generate, apply migrations, dev servers, builds, database writes, stock assignment/conversion/adjustment integration tests, storefront/browser tests, or mobile/device tests because the fast Bun monorepo rule keeps this phase to scoped static verification unless heavier gates are explicitly requested. Durable `ProductShareLinkReservation` rows, durable stock movement rows for these reservation-aware changes, reservation expiry/release jobs, and admin conflict review remain future slices.

### Retail Ops Share Links Phase 47 - Inventory Reservation Bridge
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`; `brain/api/contracts.md`; `brain/database/schema.md`; `brain/modules/merchant-system.md`
- Completed: Added the first live inventory-reservation bridge for shared product links. Public shared-link order requests now atomically reserve the selected unit by incrementing `InventoryItem.reservedQuantity` before creating the pending `Order`/`OrderItem`, persist reservation metadata on the order and line, and keep link order counters updated in the same transaction. Protected follow-up status updates now only finalize pending shared-link requests: completing a request consumes the reservation by decrementing both `reservedQuantity` and `onHandQuantity`, while cancelling releases the reservation by decrementing only `reservedQuantity`. Central POS sale creation now checks available store stock as `onHandQuantity - reservedQuantity` and uses an optimistic `reservedQuantity` guard before decrementing stock, so in-person sales do not consume stock already held by pending product-link requests.
- Changed Source Files: `packages/db/src/queries/retail-ops-share-links.ts`, `packages/db/src/queries/retail-ops-sales.ts`, `apps/api/src/trpc/routers/retail-ops.ts`.

- Checks Run: targeted Biome check with formatter disabled for the Retail Ops share-link query, sales query, and API router; targeted Bun import for the Retail Ops share-link and sales query modules; targeted Bun import for the API Retail Ops router with a placeholder `DATABASE_URL`; stale reservation wording scan.
- Skipped Checks Or Unresolved Issues: Did not run typecheck, Prisma generate, apply migrations, dev servers, builds, database writes, storefront/browser tests, mobile/device tests, or live reservation/follow-up integration tests because the fast Bun monorepo rule keeps this phase to scoped static verification unless heavier gates are explicitly requested. The router import used a placeholder `DATABASE_URL` and emitted the existing Better Auth low-entropy dev-secret warning. Durable `ProductShareLinkReservation` rows, notification audit rows, daily analytics rollups, receipt creation, payment collection, fulfillment workflow, and reservation-aware guards for stock assignment/conversion/manual decrease remain future slices.

### Retail Ops Offline Sync API Phase 1 - Idempotent Event Replay
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/plans/2026-07-06-feature-offline-first-sales-sync.md`
- Completed: Added the first production sync replay endpoint. `retailOps.syncEvents` accepts a bounded batch of offline events, requires a POS-capable tenant member, applies supported `sale_created`, `stock_intake_recorded`, and `unit_conversion_recorded` payloads through the existing idempotent mutation helpers, and returns per-event applied, failed, or skipped results. Unsupported local queue event types are skipped instead of failing the whole batch until their replay contracts are implemented.

### Retail Ops Offline Device API Phase 1 - Entitled Device Registration
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/plans/2026-07-06-feature-offline-first-sales-sync.md`; `brain/plans/2026-07-06-feature-saas-subscription-packaging.md`
- Completed: Added first-phase production offline-device registration. `retailOps.registerOfflineDevice` accepts a device id, platform, optional device name, optional app version, and optional store scope for POS-capable tenant members. The DB helper stores or refreshes metadata-backed devices under `Tenant.metadata.retailOps.offlineDevices`, counts them in the subscription snapshot, and checks the `offlineDevices` entitlement before adding a new device.

### Retail Ops Product Share-Link API Phase 1 - Metadata-Backed Links And Pending Requests
- Source Mode: Goal Implementation
- Source Brain Record: `brain/features/mobile-retail-ops-mvp-spec.md`
- Completed: Added the first production product share-link bridge. The public `retailOps.sharedProduct` procedure resolves active shared product links by tenant/store/product slug and opaque token, records a first view count, and returns web product-page data. The public `retailOps.createSharedProductOrderRequest` procedure creates a pending order request with customer details and share-link attribution, rejects over-available quantities, and enqueues customer/merchant notification dispatch. The protected `retailOps.productShareLinks`, `retailOps.createProductShareLink`, and `retailOps.deactivateProductShareLink` procedures resolve tenant/store context, allow POS-capable roles to list and create generated product URLs, store opaque token link records in product metadata, and let creators or manager-level users deactivate links without deleting history. The storefront app now renders `/p/[tenantSlug]/[storeSlug]/[productSlug]?share=...` with server metadata, a generated preview image, variant selection, customer fields, and a pending order-request form.
